vance_legacy_1 = { # Gatekeepers of the Trident
	legacy = vance_legacy_track

	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Vance
	}

	effect = { #Unlock MAA Riverward Rangers
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = vance_legacy_1_effect
		}
	}

	character_modifier = {
		additional_fort_level = 1
		archers_damage_mult = 0.10
		men_at_arms_maintenance = -0.10
	}
	ai_chance = {
		value = 100
	}

}
vance_legacy_2 = { # Honor of Atranta
	legacy = vance_legacy_track

	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Vance 
	}

	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Casterly
	}

	effect = { 
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = casterly_legacy_4_effect
		}
	}

	character_modifier = { 
		enemy_hostile_scheme_success_chance_add = -20
		monthly_intrigue_lifestyle_xp_gain_mult = 0.05
		intrigue_scheme_resistance = 15
		dread_gain_mult = 0.15  
	}
	ai_chance = {
		value = 100
	}

}

casterly_legacy_5 = { #  The First Lions
	legacy = casterly_legacy_track
	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Casterly
	}

	effect = { # Effect is applied in the on action 'on_birth_child
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = casterly_legacy_5_effect
		}
	}
	traits = {
		ambitious = 100
	}

	character_modifier = {
		knight_effectiveness_mult = 0.15
		# monthly_dynasty_prestige = 0.05
		monthly_prestige = 0.50
	}
	ai_chance = {
		value = 100
	}

}
qoherys_legacy_1 = { # Scorched Throne
	legacy = qoherys_legacy_track

	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Qoherys
	}

	effect = { #Unlocks MAA Blackened Blades
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = qoherys_legacy_1_effect
		}
	}

	character_modifier = {
		short_reign_duration_mult = -0.2
		domain_limit = 1
		build_gold_cost = -0.10  
	}
	ai_chance = {
		value = 100
	}

}

	can_be_picked = { 
		dynasty = dynasty:dynn_Vyrwel
	}

	effect = { # Effect is applied in the on action 'on_birth_child
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = vyrwel_legacy_1_effect
		}
	}

	traits = {
		diligent = 100
	}

	character_modifier = {
		domain_tax_mult = 0.05
		monthly_county_control_growth_factor = 0.10
		stress_loss_mult = 0.05 
	}
	ai_chance = {
		value = 100
	}

}
